msg:The hotel is located in the city center. If you drive there, it is located next to the main road. The building is very eye-catching. There are ground and underground parking lots, but the underground parking lot is relatively small and dimly lit. There are many ground parking spaces, which is convenient. The hotel has a grand lobby and warm front desk service. We have a lot of people and luggage, so we need to use the hotel's luggage cart. The lobby staff took the initiative to help push the cart and move it to the room. The service is good. The room is spacious, the twin bed of 1.35 meters is very comfortable, the bathroom is separated into dry and wet areas, the hotel room is equipped with a refrigerator, complete facilities, clean and sanitary, customer service, and they take the initiative to replenish the free supplies every day, and they also leave two more free bottles of bottled water, with a strong sense of proactive service. There is a heated swimming pool and gym on the 6th floor of the hotel. We like to swim as a family. The swimming pool is open until 8 pm. Although the swimming pool is a little small, the water quality is good and the water is kept at a constant temperature. Locals hold wedding banquets in this hotel, and there are many children's banquets, so it should be a good hotel in the local area. The hotel breakfast is good from a distance. Because we are not people who like to eat buffets, we did not try it. I will not comment here, but there are many restaurants around the hotel, and there are some special breakfast shops. We will try the local characteristics every time we go to a city. The nearby restaurants are basically fusion dishes, among which mutton soup and mixed noodles are also good. The hotel is not far from the attractions in Bozhou, and it can be reached in about 10 to 20 minutes by car. Cao Cao's Underground Transport Road and Huaxilou are the two main attractions. The Transport Road is indeed good and feels like the best attraction. The hotel is good in all aspects and is worth recommending.
